will be reduced to\u00a080\u00a0% of basic duty, i.e. 8\u00a0%;\n\n\n(c)\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0on\u00a01\u00a0January of the fourth year following the date of entry into force of this Agreement, the import duty will be reduced to\u00a070\u00a0% of basic duty, i.e. 7\u00a0%;\n\n\n(d)\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0on\u00a01\u00a0January of the fifth year following the date of entry into force of this Agreement, the import duty will be reduced to\u00a060\u00a0% of basic duty, i.e. 6\u00a0%;\n\n\n(e)\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0on\u00a01\u00a0January of the sixth year following the date of entry into force of this Agreement, the import duty will be reduced to\u00a050\u00a0% of basic duty, i.e. 5\u00a0%;\n\n\n(f)\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0on\u00a01\u00a0January of the seventh year following the date of entry into force of this Agreement, the import duty will be reduced to\u00a030\u00a0% of basic duty, i.e. 3\u00a0%;\n\n\n(g)\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0on\u00a01\u00a0January of the eighth year following the date of entry into force of this Agreement, the import duty will be reduced to\u00a010\u00a0% of basic duty, i.e. 1\u00a0%;\n\n\n(h)\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0on\u00a01\u00a0January of the ninth year following the date of entry into force of this Agreement, the remaining import duties will be abolished.\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nCode\n\n\n\n\nDescription\n6\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n0701\n\n\n\n\nPotatoes, fresh or Article\u00a050\n\n\n\n\n\nFINANCIAL SERVICES: DEFINITIONS\n\n\n\nA financial service is any service of a financial nature offered by a financial service provider of a Party.\n\n\n\nFinancial services include the following activities:\n\n\n\nA.\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0All Insurance and insurancerelated services:\n\n\n1.\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0direct insurance (including coinsurance):\n\n\n(a)\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0life;\n\n\n(b)\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0nonlife;\n\n\n2.\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0reinsurance and retrocession;\n\n\n3.\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0insurance intermediation, such as brokerage and agency;\n\n\n4.\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0services auxiliary to insurance, such as consultancy, actuarial, risk assessment and claim settlement services.\n\n\n\nB.\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0Banking and other financial services (excluding insurance):\n\n\n1.\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0acceptance of deposits and other repayable funds from the public;\n\n\n2.\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0lending of all types, including, inter alia, consumercredit, mortgage credit, factoring and financing of commercial transaction;\n\n\n3.\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0financial leasing;\n\n\n4.\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0all payment and money transmission services, including credit, charge and debit cards, travellers cheques and bankers drafts;\n\n\n5.\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0guarantees and commitments;\n\n\n6.\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0trading for own account or for account of customers, whether on an exchange, in an over the counter market or otherwise, the following:\n\n\n\n\n(a)\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0money market instruments (cheques, bills, certificates of deposits);\n\n\n(b)\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0foreign exchange;\n\n\n(c)\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0derivative products including, but not limited to, futures and options;\n\n\n(d)\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0exchange rates and interest rate instruments, including products such as swaps and forward rate agreements;\n\n\n(e)\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0transferable securities;\n\n\n(f)\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0other negotiable instruments and financial assets, including bullion.\n\n\n7.\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0participation in issues of all kinds of securities, including underwriting and placement as agent (whether publicly or privately) and provision of services related to such issues;\n\n\n8.\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0money broking;\n\n\n9.\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0asset management, such as cash or portfolio management, all forms of collective investment management, pensionfund management, custodial, depository and trust services;\n\n\n10.\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0settlement and clearing services for financial assets, including securities, derivative products, and other negotiable instruments;\n\n\n11.\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0provision and transfer of financial information, and processing of financial data and related software by providers of other financial services;\n\n\n12.\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0advisory, intermediation and other auxiliary financial services on all the activities listed in points\u00a01 to\u00a011, including credit reference and analysis, investment and portfolio research and advice, advice on acquisitions and on corporate restructuring and strategy.\n\n\n\nThe following activities are excluded from the definition of financial services:\n\n\n(a)\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0activities carried out by central banks or by any other public institution in pursuit of monetary and exchange rate policies;\n\n\n(b)\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0activities conducted by central banks, government agencies or departments, or public institutions, for the account or with the guarantee of the government, except when those activities may be carried out by financial service providers in competition with such public entities;\n\n\n(c)\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0activities forming part of a statutory system of social security or public retirement plans, except when those activities may be carried by financial service providers in competition with public entities or private institutions.\n\n\n\nThe SAC may extend or modify the scope of this Annex.\n\n\n\n\n\n\n________________\n\n\n\n\nANNEX VII\n\n\n\n\nINTELLECTUAL, INDUSTRIAL AND COMMERCIAL PROPERTY RIGHTS\n\n\nReferred to in for a\nCOUNCIL DECISION\non the signing, on behalf of the European Union, of the Stabilisation and Association Agreement between the European Union and the European Atomic Energy Community, of the one part, and of Kosovo*, of the other part \n\n\n\n\n\n\nEXPLANATORY MEMORANDUM\n\n\n1.CONTEXT OF THE PROPOSAL\n\n\nIn June 2013, the Council authorised the Commission to open negotiations with Kosovo\n1*\u00a0on an EU-only Stabilisation and Association Agreement and adopted negotiating directives. There were three formal rounds of negotiations. The first round was held on 28 October 2013, the second on 27 November 2013 and the third on 2 May 2014. The chief negotiators initialled the draft text of the agreement on 25 July 2014. \n\n\nIn the attachment to this proposal, the Commission presents the initialled text of the Stabilisation and Association Agreement with Kosovo. The draft agreement is modelled on similar examples from the region, while taking into consideration the EU-only nature of the agreement and the specificities of Kosovo. In this context, it is important to underline that a Stabilisation and Association Agreement between the EU and Kosovo can be signed in a way that respects the positions of Member States on the status of Kosovo.\n\n\n2.RESULTS OF CONSULTATIONS WITH THE INTERESTED PARTIES AND IMPACT ASSESSMENTS\n\n\nThis proposal is the result of extensive negotiations between the Union, on one side, and Kosovo, on the other. The Stabilisation and Association Agreement with Kosovo provides for wide-ranging cooperation. It provides for a framework for political dialogue with Kosovo, both at a bilateral and regional level. The agreement promotes regional cooperation and Kosovo makes a strong commitment in the agreement to the normalisation of relations with Serbia. \n\n\nThe deepening of economic and trade relations is one of the main goals of the agreement. The agreement sets out the perspective of establishing a free trade area covering goods and services, consistent with the relevant WTO principles, after a transitional period in specific areas. The length of the transitional period was established during the negotiations in light of the state of preparation of Kosovo. \n\n\nThe agreement also includes provisions on establishment, supply of services, current payments and movement of capital. It includes the commitment by Kosovo to progressively harmonise its legislation with that of the EU, notably in key areas of the internal market. It establishes relations covering almost all areas of EU interest and provides a basis for wide-ranging cooperation. Overall, the cooperation is underpinned by EU financial and technical assistance, which provides Kosovo with the necessary support and assistance in the implementation of certain aspects of the agreement.\n\n\nDuring all stages of the negotiations, the negotiator regularly consulted the special committee designated by the Council (COWEB). \n\n\n3.LEGAL ELEMENTS OF THE PROPOSAL\n\n\nThe legal basis for the signature of this agreement is Article 217, in conjunction with Article 218(5) and the second subparagraph of Article 218(8) of the Treaty on the Functioning of the European Union. \n\n\nFollowing the judgement in case C-377/12 Commission v. Council, the Commission considers that the Stabilisation and Association Agreement can be signed in one single act.\n\n\nA separate legal instrument applies to the European Atomic Energy Community.\n\n\n2015/0095 (NLE)\n\n\nProposal for a\n\n\nCOUNCIL DECISION\n\n\non the signing, on behalf of the European Union, of the Stabilisation and Association Agreement between the European Union and the European Atomic Energy Community, of the one part, and of Kosovo\n2*, of the other part \n\n\nTHE COUNCIL OF THE EUROPEAN UNION,\u00a0\n\n\nHaving regard to the Treaty on the Functioning of the European Union, and in particular Article 217, in conjunction with Article 218(5) and the second subparagraph of Article 218(8) thereof,\n\n\n\n\nHaving regard to the proposal from the European Commission,\n\n\nWhereas: \n\n\n(1)On 21 June 2013 the Council authorised the Commission to open negotiations with Kosovo for a Stabilisation and Association Agreement. The negotiations were successfully concluded by the initialling of the Agreement on 25 July 2014.\n\n\n(2)The EU and Kosovo have strong links and share values and a desire to strengthen those links and establish a close and lasting relationship based on reciprocity and mutual interest, which should allow Kosovo to further strengthen and extend its relations with the EU.\n\n\n(3)The \"First agreement on principles governing the normalisation of relations\" was reached on 19 April 2013 in the framework of the EUfacilitated dialogue.\n\n\n(4)The Agreement as initialled provides for the establishment of an association between the EU and Kosovo involving reciprocal rights and obligations, common actions and special procedure. The decision to sign this Agreement should therefore be based on the legal basis providing for the establishment of an association allowing the Union to enter into commitments in all areas covered by the Treaties.\n\n\n(5)This is an EU-only agreement. Next to setting up an association and providing for a framework of political dialogue, the agreement as initialled envisages the granting of rights and obligations in the area of common commercial policy. Furthermore, it contains provisions regarding various policies in which the Union shares competence with Member States and which fall within areas already largely covered by common Union rules. In addition, it provides for wide-ranging cooperation in various policy areas, including in justice and home affairs, which is limited to what is characteristic for technical, financial and economic cooperation. \n\n\n(6)The signature of the Stabilisation and Association Agreement is without prejudice to Member\u00a0States' position on the status of Kosovo, which will be decided in accordance with their national practice and international law.\n\n\n(7)In addition, none of the terms,  wording or definitions used in this  Decision and the attached text of the Agreement, nor any recourse to all the necessary legal bases for the signature of the Agreement constitute recognition of Kosovo by the Union as an independent State nor does it constitute recognition by individual Member\u00a0States of Kosovo in that capacity where they have not taken such a step. It is appropriate, in that context that a declaration is issued in that regard by the Union at the moment of signing of this Agreement. \n\n\n(8)The signature of the Agreement as regards matters falling under the competence of the European Atomic Energy Community is subject to a separate procedure.\n\n\n(9)The Agreement should therefore be signed on behalf of the European Union, subject to its conclusion at a later date,\n\n\nHAS ADOPTED THIS DECISION: \n\n\nArticle 1\n\n\nThe signing, on behalf of the European Union, of the Stabilisation and Association Agreement between the European Union and the European Atomic Energy Community, of the one part, and of Kosovo*, of the other part, is hereby approved for the parts falling under the Treaty on European Union and the Treaty on the Functioning of the European Union subject to the conclusion of the said Agreement. \n\n\nThe text of the Agreement to be signed is attached to this Decision.\n\n\nThe signature of the Agreement as regards matters falling under the competence of the European Atomic Energy Community is subject to a separate procedure.\n\n\nArticle 2\n\n\nThe Declaration on behalf of the European Union attached to this Decision is hereby approved on behalf of the Union. \n\n\nArticle 3\n\n\nThe present Decision is without prejudice to Member States' and the Union's position on the status of Kosovo. \n\n\n\n\nArticle 4\n\n\nThe Council Secretariat General shall establish the instrument of full powers to sign the Agreement, subject to its conclusion, for the person(s) indicated by the negotiator of the Agreement.\n\n\nArticle 5\n\n\nThis Decision shall enter into force on [\u2026].\n\n\nDone at Brussels,\n\n\n\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0For the Council\n\n\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0The President\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n(1)\n*\u00a0This designation is without prejudice to positions on status, and is in line with UNSCR 1244/1999 and the ICJ Opinion on the Kosovo declaration of independence.\n\n\n\n(2)\n*\u00a0This designation is without prejudice to positions on status, and is in line with UNSCR 1244/1999 and the ICJ Opinion on the Kosovo declaration of independence.\n\n\n\n\n\nTop  \n\n\n\n\n\n\nEUROPEAN COMMISSION\nBrussels, 30.4.2015\nCOM(2015) 183 final\nANNEX\n\nto the Proposal for a\nCOUNCIL DECISION\non the signing, on behalf of the European Union, of the Stabilisation and Association Agreement between the European Union and the European Atomic Energy Community, of the one part, and of Kosovo*, of the other part \n\n\n\n\n\n\nDeclaration on behalf of the Union\n\n\nThe decision to sign the Stabilisation and Association Agreement subject to its conclusion at a later date, including the legal bases used in that regard, is without prejudice to Member States' positions on status and does not constitute recognition of Kosovo\n1* by the Union as an independent State, nor does it constitute recognition by individual Member States in that capacity where they have not previously taken such a step.\n\n\n\n\n\n\n(1)\n*\u00a0This designation is without prejudice to positions on status, and is in line with UNSCR\u00a01244/1999 and the ICJ Opinion on the Kosovo declaration of independence.\n\n\n\n\n\nTop  \n\n\n\n\n\n\nEUROPEAN COMMISSION\nBrussels, 30.4.2015\nCOM(2015) 183 final\nANNEX\n\nto the Proposal for a\nCOUNCIL DECISION\non the signing, on behalf of the European Union, of the Stabilisation and Association Agreement between the European Union and the European Atomic Energy Community, of the one part, and of Kosovo*, of the other part \n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nSTABILISATION AND ASSOCIATION AGREEMENT\n\n\nBETWEEN THE EUROPEAN UNION, OF THE ONE PART,\n\n\nAND KOSOVO\n1*, OF THE OTHER PART\n\n\n\nTHE EUROPEAN UNION, hereinafter referred to as \u201cthe Union\u201d or \u201cthe EU\u201d, and THE EUROPEAN ATOMIC ENERGY COMMUNITY,\n\n\n\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0of the one part, and\n\n\n\nKOSOVO\n2*,\n\n\n\n\n\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0of the other part,\n\n\n\nhereinafter jointly referred to as \u201cthe Parties\u201d,\n\n\n\n\nCONSIDERING the strong links between the Parties and the values that they share, their desire to strengthen those links and establish a close and lasting relationship based on reciprocity and mutual interest, which should allow Kosovo to further strengthen and extend its relations with the EU;\n\n\n\nCONSIDERING the importance of this Agreement, in the framework of the Stabilisation and Association Process (SAP) with the Western Balkans, in the establishment and consolidation of a stable European order based on cooperation, of which the EU is a mainstay;\n\n\n\nCONSIDERING the EU\u2019s readiness to take concrete steps to realise Kosovo\u2019s European perspective and rapprochement with the EU in line with the perspective of the region by integrating Kosovo towards the political and economic mainstream of Europe, through Kosovo\u2019s ongoing participation in the SAP with the aim to fulfil the relevant criteria and SAP conditionalities, subject to the successful implementation of this Agreement, notably regarding regional cooperation; this process will lead to progress in Kosovo\u2019s European perspective and rapprochement with the EU, should objective circumstances so permit and Kosovo fulfil the criteria defined by the European Council in Copenhagen on\u00a02122\u00a0June\u00a01993 and the aforementioned conditionalities;\n\n\n\nCONSIDERING the commitment of the Parties to contribute by appropriate means to the political, economic and institutional stabilisation in Kosovo as well as in the region, through the development of civil society and democratisation, institution building and public administration reform, regional trade integration and enhanced economic cooperation, wide ranging cooperation, including in justice and home affairs, and the strengthening of security;\n\n\n\nCONSIDERING the commitment of the Parties to increasing political and economic freedoms as the very basis of this Agreement, as well as their commitment to respect human rights, including the rights of persons belonging to minorities and vulnerable groups,\n\n\n\nCONSIDERING the commitment of the Parties to institutions based on the rule of law, to good governance and democratic principles through a multiparty system with free and fair elections;\n\n\n\nCONSIDERING the commitment of the Parties to respect the principles of the Charter of the United Nations, of the Organisation for Security and Cooperation in Europe (OSCE), notably those of t he Final Act of the Conference on Security and Cooperation in Europe of\u00a01975 (hereinafter referred to as \u201cthe Helsinki Final Act\u201d) and the Charter of Paris for a New Europe of\u00a01990;\n\n\n\nREAFFIRMING the attachment of the Parties to the implementation of international obligations, in particular but not only, related to the protection of human rights and the protection of persons belonging to minorities and vulnerable groups and in this respect noting the commitment of Kosovo to abide by the relevant international instruments;\n\n\n\n\n\nREAFFIRMING the right of return for all refugees and internally displaced persons and to the protection of their property and other related human rights;\n\n\n\nCONSIDERING the commitment of the Parties to the principles of the free market economy and to sustainable development as well as the readiness of the EU to contribute to the economic reforms in Kosovo;\n\n\n\nCONSIDERING the commitment of the Parties to free trade, consistent with the relevant principles of the World Trade Organisation (hereinafter referred to as \u201cWTO\u201d) which are to be applied in a transparent and nondiscriminatory manner;\n\n\n\nCONSIDERING the commitment of the Parties to further develop regular political dialogue on issues of mutual interest, including regional aspects;\n\n\n\nCONSIDERING the importance the Parties attach to combating organised crime, corruption and to strengthening cooperation in the fight against terrorism in line with the EU acquis, and to preventing irregular migration while supporting mobility in a legal and secure environment;\n\n\n\nCONVINCED that this Agreement will create a new climate for economic relations between the Parties and, above all, for the development of trade and investment, factors crucial to economic restructuring and modernisation;\n\n\n\nBEARING in mind the commitment by Kosovo to approximate its legislation in the relevant sectors to that of the EU, and to effectively implement it;\n\n\n\nTAKING ACCOUNT of the EU\u2019s willingness to provide decisive support for the implementation of reform and to use all available instruments of cooperation and technical, financial and economic assistance on a comprehensive indicative multiannual basis to this endeavour, should objective circumstances so permit;\n\n\n\nNOTING that this Agreement is without prejudice to positions on status, and is in line with UNSCR\u00a01244/1999 and the ICJ Opinion on the Kosovo declaration of independence;\n\n\n\nNOTING that the internal procedures of the Member\u00a0States of the European Union (hereinafter referred to as the \u201cMember\u00a0States\u201d) may apply when receiving documents issued by Kosovo authorities under this Agreement;\n\n\n\nNOTING that negotiations are ongoing for the establishment of a Transport Community with the Western Balkans;\n\n\n\n\n\nRECALLING the Zagreb Summit of\u00a02000, which called for further consolidation of relations through the SAP as well as enhanced regional cooperation;\n\n\n\nRECALLING that the European Council in Thessaloniki on\u00a019 and\u00a020\u00a0June\u00a02003 reinforced the SAP as the policy framework for the EU\u2019s relations with the Western Balkans and underlined the prospect of integration with the EU on the basis of their individual reform progress and merit;\n\n\n\nRECALLING Kosovo\u2019s commitments in the context of the Central European Free Trade Agreement, signed in Bucharest on\u00a019.12.2006, concluded with the aim to enhance the region\u2019s ability to attract investments and the prospects of its integration into the global economy, should objective circumstances so permit;\n\n\n\nDESIROUS of establishing closer cultural cooperation and developing exchanges of information,\n\n\n\nNOTING that in case the Parties decided, within the framework of this Agreement, to enter into specific agreements in the Area of Freedom, Security and Justice which were to be concluded by the EU pursuant to Title\u00a0V of Part Three of the Treaty on the Functioning of the European Union, the provisions of such future specific agreements would not bind the United Kingdom and/or Ireland unless the EU, simultaneously with the United Kingdom and/or Ireland as regards their respective previous bilateral relations, notifies Kosovo that the United Kingdom and/or Ireland has/have become bound by such future specific agreements as part of the EU in accordance with Protocol No\u00a021 on the position of the United Kingdom and Ireland in respect of the area of Freedom, Security and Justice annexed to the Treaty on European Union and to the Treaty on the Functioning of the European Union. Likewise, any subsequent EUinternal measures which were to be adopted pursuant to the above mentioned Title\u00a0V to implement this Agreement would not bind the United Kingdom and/or Ireland unless they have notified their wish to take part in or accept such measures in accordance with Protocol No\u00a021. Also noting that such future specific agreements or such subsequent EUinternal measures would fall within Protocol No\u00a022 on the position of Denmark annexed to those Treaties.\n\n\n\nHAVE AGREED AS FOLLOWS:\n\n\n\nARTICLE 1\n\n\n\n1.\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0An association is hereby established between the EU, of the one part, and Kosovo, of the other part.\n\n\n\n2.\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0The aims of this association are:\n\n\n\n(a)\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0to support the efforts of Kosovo to strengthen democracy and the rule of law;\n\n\n\n(b)\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0to contribute to political, economic and institutional stability in Kosovo, as well as to the stabilisation of the region;\n\n\n\n\n\n(c)\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0to provide an appropriate framework for political dialogue, allowing the development of close political relations between the Parties;\n\n\n\n(d)\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0to support the efforts of Kosovo to develop its economic and international cooperation, should objective circumstances so permit, including through the approximation of its legislation to that of the EU;\n\n\n\n(e)\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0to support the efforts of Kosovo to complete the transition into a functioning market economy;\n\n\n\n(f)\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0to promote harmonious economic relations and gradually develop a free trade area between the EU and Kosovo;\n\n\n\n(g)\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0to foster regional cooperation in all the fields covered by this Agreement.\n\n\n\n\nARTICLE 2\n\n\n\nNone of the terms, wording or definitions used in this Agreement, including the Annexes and Protocols thereto, constitute recognition of Kosovo by the EU as an independent State nor does it constitute recognition by individual Member\u00a0States of Kosovo in that capacity where they have not taken such a step.\n\n\n\nTITLE I\n\n\n\nGENERAL PRINCIPLES\n\n\n\n\nARTICLE 3\n\n\n\n\n\nRespect for the democratic principles and human rights as proclaimed in the United Nations Universal Declaration of Human Rights of\u00a01948 and as defined in the Convention for the Protection of Human Rights and Fundamental Freedoms of\u00a01950, in the Helsinki Final Act and the Charter of Paris for a New Europe, respect for international law principles, including full cooperation with the International Criminal Tribunal for the former Yugoslavia (ICTY) and its residual mechanism, the International Criminal Court, and respect for the rule of law as well as the principles of market economy as reflected in the Document of the Bonn Conference on Economic Cooperation of the Conference on Security Cooperation in Europe, shall form the basis of the policies of the EU and of Kosovo and constitute essential elements of this Agreement.\n\n\n\nARTICLE 4\n\n\n\nKosovo commits to abide by international law and instruments, in particular, but not only, related to the protection of human and fundamental rights, to the protection of persons belonging to minorities, and without discrimination on any ground.\n\n\n\n\nARTICLE 5\n\n\n\nKosovo commits to continued engagement towards a visible and sustainable improvement in relations with Serbia and to effective cooperation with the Common Security and Defence Policy mission while in place, as further defined in Article\u00a013. These commitments constitute essential principles of this Agreement and shall underpin the development of relations and cooperation between the Parties. In case of the noncompliance by Kosovo with these commitments, the EU may take measures it deems appropriate, including suspending all or part of this Agreement.\n\n\n\nARTICLE 6\n\n\n\nThe Parties reaffirm that the most serious crimes of concern to the international community as a whole should not go unpunished and that prosecution of these crimes should be ensured by taking measures at domestic and international level.\n\n\n\nIn this respect, Kosovo undertakes, in particular, to fully cooperate with the ICTY and its residual mechanism, and all other investigations and prosecutions conducted under international auspices.\n\n\n\nKosovo also undertakes to abide by the Rome Statute of the International Criminal Court and in this respect to take the necessary steps for its implementation at domestic level.\n\n\n\n\nARTICLE 7\n\n\n\n\n\nThe development of regional cooperation and good neighbourly relations as well as respect for human rights, including the rights of persons belonging to minorities, are central to the SAP. The conclusion and the implementation of this Agreement takes place within the framework of the SAP and are based on Kosovo\u2019s own merits .\n\n\n\nARTICLE 8\n\n\n\nKosovo commits to continue to foster cooperation and good neighbourly relations in the region including an appropriate level of mutual concessions concerning the movement of persons, goods, capital and services as well as the development of projects of common interest in a wide range of areas, including the rule of law. This commitment constitutes a key factor in the development of relations and cooperation between the Parties, thus contributing to regional stability.\n\n\n\n\nARTICLE 9\n\n\n\nThe association shall be progressively and fully realised over a period of ten years.\n\n\n\nThe Stabilisation and Association Council (hereinafter referred to as \u201cSAC\u201d) established under Article\u00a0126 shall review, on an annual basis, the implementation of this Agreement and the adoption and implementation by Kosovo of legal, administrative, institutional and economic reforms. This review shall be carried out in the light of the preamble and in accordance with the general principles of this Agreement. It shall be consistent with the mechanisms established under the SAP, notably the progress report on the SAP.\n\n\n\nOn the basis of this review, the SAC will issue recommendations and may take decisions.\n\n\n\nWhere the review identifies particular difficulties, they may be referred to the dispute settlement mechanisms established under this Agreement.\n\n\n\nNo later than the fifth year after the entry into force of this Agreement, the SAC shall make a thorough review of the implementation of this Agreement. On the basis of this review the SAC shall evaluate progress made by Kosovo and may take decisions governing the ensuing process of association. Similar steps shall be taken by the SAC before the end of the tenth year after the entry into force of this Agreement. If warranted by the results of the review, the SAC may take a decision to extend the period set out in paragraph\u00a01 by not more than five years. In the absence of such decisions by the SAC, this Agreement shall continue to be implemented as agreed herein.\n\n\n\nThe aforementioned review shall not apply to the free movement of goods, for which a specific schedule is provided for in Title\u00a0IV.\n\n\n\n\n\n\nARTICLE 10\n\n\n\nThis Agreement shall be fully compatible, and implemented in a manner consistent with the relevant provisions contained in the WTO Agreements, in particular Article XXIV of the General Agreement on Tariffs and Trade\u00a01994 (GATT\u00a01994) and Article V of the General Agreement on Trade in Services (GATS).\n\n\n\nTITLE II\n\n\n\nPOLITICAL DIALOGUE\n\n\n\n\nARTICLE 11\n\n\n\n1.\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0Political dialogue between the Parties shall be further developed within the context of this Agreement. It shall accompany and consolidate the rapprochement between the EU and Kosovo and contribute to the establishment of close links of solidarity and new forms of cooperation between the Parties.\n\n\n\n2.\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0The political dialogue is intended to promote in particular:\n\n\n\n(a)\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0Kosovo\u2019s participation in the international democratic community, should objective circumstances so permit;\n\n\n\n(b)\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0advancement of Kosovo\u2019s European perspective and rapprochement with the EU, in line with the European perspective of the region, based on individual merits and in line with Kosovo\u2019s commitments under Article\u00a05 of this Agreement;\n\n\n\n(c)\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0increasing convergence with certain Common Foreign and Security Policy measures, particular restrictive measures taken by the EU against third countries, natural or legal persons or nonState entities also through the exchange of information as appropriate, and, in particular, on those issues likely to have substantial effects on the Parties;\n\n\n\n(d)\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0effective, inclusive and representative regional cooperation and the development of good neighbourly relations in the Western Balkans.\n\n\n\n\n\n\nARTICLE 12\n\n\n\nThe Parties shall have a policy dialogue on the other issues covered by this Agreement.\n\n\n\n\nARTICLE 13\n\n\n\n1.\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0Political dialogue and policy dialogue, as appropriate, contribute to the process of normalisation of relations between Kosovo and Serbia.\n\n\n\n2.\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0As provided for in Article\u00a05, Kosovo commits to continued engagement towards a visible and sustainable improvement in relations with Serbia. This process shall ensure that both can continue on their respective European paths, while avoiding that either can block the other in these efforts, and should gradually lead to the comprehensive normalisation of relations between Kosovo and Serbia, in the form of a legally binding agreement, with the prospect of both being able to fully exercise their rights and fulfil their responsibilities.\n\n\n\n3.\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0In the above framework, Kosovo shall continuously:\n\n\n\n(a)\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0implement in good faith all agreements reached in the dialogue with Serbia;\n\n\n\n(b)\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0fully respect the principles of inclusive regional cooperation;\n\n\n\n(c)\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0resolve through dialogue and a spirit of compromise other outstanding issues, on the basis of practical and sustainable solutions and cooperate on the necessary technical and legal matters with Serbia;\n\n\n\n\n\n(d)\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0cooperate effectively with the Common Security and Defence Policy mission while in place and contribute actively to a full and unhindered execution of its mandate throughout Kosovo.\n\n\n\n4.\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0The SAC shall regularly review the progress in this process, and may take decisions and issue recommendations in this regard. The Stabilisation and Association Committee may assist this process in accordance with Article\u00a0129.\n\n\n\n\nARTICLE 14\n\n\n\n1.\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0Political and policy dialogues shall primarily take place within the SAC, which shall have the general responsibility for any matter which the Parties might wish to put to it.\n\n\n\n2.\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0At the request of any of the Parties, these dialogues may also take place in the following formats:\n\n\n\n(a)\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0meetings, where necessary, of senior officials representing Kosovo, on the one hand, and the High Representative of the Union for Foreign Affairs and Security Policy and/or a representative of the Commission, on the other;\n\n\n\n(b)\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0taking full advantage of all appropriate channels between the Parties, including appropriate contacts in nonEU countries and within international organisations and other international fora, should objective circumstances so permit;\n\n\n\n(c)\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0any other means which would make a useful contribution to consolidating, developing and stepping up these dialogues, including those identified in the Thessaloniki agenda, adopted in the Conclusions of the European Council in Thessaloniki on\u00a019 and\u00a020\u00a0June\u00a02003.\n\n\n\n\nARTICLE 15\n\n\n\nA political dialogue at parliamentary level shall take place within the framework of the Stabilisation and Association Parliamentary Committee established under Article\u00a0132.\n\n\n\nTITLE III\n\n\n\n\n\nREGIONAL COOPERATION\n\n\n\n\nARTICLE 16\n\n\n\nIn conformity with its commitment under Articles\u00a05 and\u00a013, and to international and regional peace and stability, and to the development of good neighbourly relations, Kosovo shall actively promote regional cooperation. The EU, through appropriate instruments, including assistance to projects having a regional or crossborder/boundary dimension, may support these efforts.\n\n\n\nWhenever Kosovo plans to reinforce its cooperation with one of the countries referred to in Articles\u00a017, 18 and\u00a019, it shall inform and consult the EU in accordance with the provisions laid down in Title\u00a0X.\n\n\n\nKosovo shall continue to implement the Central European Free Trade Agreement.\n\n\n\n\nARTICLE 17\n\n\n\nCooperation with countries \nhaving signed a Stabilisation and Association Agreement\n\n\n\nAfter the signature of this Agreement, Kosovo shall, should objective circumstances so permit, start negotiations with the countries which have already signed a Stabilisation and Association Agreement with the EU with a view to concluding bilateral conventions on regional cooperation, the aim of which shall be to enhance the scope of cooperation between them.\n\n\n\nThe main elements of these conventions shall be:\n\n\n\n(a)\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0political dialogue;\n\n\n\n\n\n(b)\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0the establishment of free trade areas, consistent with relevant WTO provisions;\n\n\n\n(c)\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0mutual concessions concerning the movement of workers, establishment, supply of services, current payments and movement of capital as well as other policies related to the movement of persons at an equivalent level to that of the Stabilisation and Association Agreements which that respective country has concluded with the EU;\n\n\n\n(d)\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0provisions on cooperation in other fields whether or not covered by this Agreement, and notably the field of Freedom, Security and Justice.\n\n\n\nThese conventions shall contain provisions for the creation of the necessary institutional mechanisms, as appropriate.\n\n\n\nThe conventions shall be concluded within two years after the entry into force of this Agreement.\n\n\n\n\nARTICLE 18\n\n\n\nCooperation with countries \nconcerned by the SAP\n\n\n\nKosovo shall pursue regional cooperation with countries concerned by the SAP in some or all the fields of cooperation covered by this Agreement as well as other areas related to the SAP, notably those of common interest. Such cooperation should always be compatible with the principles and objectives of this Agreement.\n\n\n\n\nARTICLE 19\n\n\n\nCooperation with candidate countries \nfor EU accession not concerned by the SAP\n\n\n\n\n\nKosovo shall foster its cooperation and conclude, should objective circumstances so permit, conventions on cooperation with any country candidate for EU accession not concerned by the SAP in the fields of cooperation covered by this Agreement and other areas of mutual interest for Kosovo and these countries. Such conventions should aim to gradually align bilateral relations between Kosovo and those countries to the relevant part of the relations between the EU and Kosovo.\n\n\n\nTITLE IV\n\n\n\nFREE MOVEMENT OF GOODS\n\n\n\n\nARTICLE 20\n\n\n\n1.\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0The EU and Kosovo shall gradually establish a bilateral free trade area over a period lasting a maximum of\u00a010 years starting from the entry into force of this Agreement in accordance with this Agreement and in conformity with the GATT\u00a01994 and the provisions contained in the relevant WTO agreements. In so doing they shall take into account the specific requirements laid down in paragraphs\u00a02 to\u00a06 of this Article.\n\n\n\n2.\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0The Combined Nomenclature shall be applied to the classification of goods in trade between the Parties.\n\n\n\n3.\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0For the purpose of this Agreement customs duties and charges having equivalent effect to customs duties include any duty or charge of any kind imposed in connection with the importation or exportation of a good, including any form of surtax or surcharge in connection with such importation or exportation, but do not include any:\n\n\n\n(a)\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0charges equivalent to an internal tax imposed consistently with paragraph\u00a02 of Article\u00a0III of the GATT\u00a01994;\n\n\n\n(b)\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0antidumping or countervailing measures;\n\n\n\n(c)\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0fees or charges commensurate with the costs of services rendered.\n\n\n\n4.\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0For each product, the basic duty to which the successive tariff reductions set out in this Agreement are to be applied shall be:\n\n\n\n\n\n(a)\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0For the EU, the EU Common Customs Tariff, established pursuant to Council Regulation (EEC) No\u00a02658/87\n3\n actually applied erga omnes on the day of the signature of this Agreement;\n\n\n\n(b)\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0For Kosovo, the tariff applied by Kosovo as of\u00a031\u00a0December\u00a02013.\n\n\n\n5.\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0If, after the signature of this Agreement, any tariff reduction is applied on an erga omnes basis, such reduced duties shall replace the basic duty referred to in paragraph\u00a04 as from the date when such reductions are applied.\n\n\n\n6.\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0The EU and Kosovo shall communicate to each other their respective basic duties and any changes thereof.\n\n\n\n\nCHAPTER I\n\n\n\nINDUSTRIAL PRODUCTS\n\n\n\n\nARTICLE 21\n\n\n\nDefinition\n\n\n\n1.\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0This Chapter shall apply to products originating in the EU or in Kosovo listed in Chapters\u00a025 to\u00a097 of the Combined Nomenclature, with the exception of the products listed in Annex\u00a0I, paragraph\u00a0I, point\u00a0(ii) of the WTO Agreement on Agriculture.\n\n\n\n2.\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0Trade between the Parties in products covered by the Treaty establishing the European Atomic Energy Community shall be conducted in accordance with that Treaty.\n\n\n\n\n\n\nARTICLE 22\n\n\n\nEU concessions on industrial products\n\n\n\n1.\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0Customs duties on imports into the EU and charges having equivalent effect shall be abolished, upon the entry into force of this Agreement, on industrial products originating in Kosovo.\n\n\n\nQuantitative restrictions on imports into the EU and measures having equivalent effect shall be abolished, upon the entry into force of this Agreement, on industrial products originating in Kosovo.\n\n\n\nARTICLE 23\n\n\n\nKosovo\u2019s concessions on industrial products\n\n\n\n1.\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0Customs duties on imports into Kosovo of industrial products originating in the EU other than those listed in Annex\u00a0I shall be abolished upon the entry into force of this Agreement.\n\n\n\n2.\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0Charges having equivalent effect to customs duties on imports into Kosovo shall be abolished, upon the entry into force of this Agreement, on industrial products originating in the EU.\n\n\n\n3.\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0Customs duties on imports into Kosovo of industrial products originating in the EU which are listed in Annex\u00a0I shall be progressively reduced and abolished in accordance with the timetable indicated in that Annex.\n\n\n\n4.\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0Quantitative restrictions on imports into Kosovo of industrial products originating in the EU and measures having equivalent effect shall be abolished upon the entry into force of this Agreement.\n\n\n\n\n\nARTICLE 24\n\n\n\nDuties and restrictions on exports\n\n\n\n1.\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0The EU and Kosovo shall abolish any customs duties on exports and charges having equivalent effect in trade between them upon the entry into force of this Agreement.\n\n\n\n2.\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0The EU and Kosovo shall abolish between themselves any quantitative restrictions on exports and measures having equivalent effect upon the entry into force of this Agreement.\n\n\n\n\nARTICLE 25\n\n\n\nFaster reductions in customs duties\n\n\n\nKosovo declares its readiness to reduce its customs duties in trade with the EU more rapidly than is provided for in Article\u00a023 if its general economic situation and the situation of the economic sector concerned so permit.\n\n\n\nThe SAC shall analyse the situation in this respect and make the relevant recommendations.\n\n\n\nCHAPTER II\n\n\n\nAGRICULTURE AND FISHERIES\n\n\n\n\n\n\nARTICLE 26\n\n\n\nDefinition\n\n\n\n1.\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0This Chapter shall apply to trade in agricultural and fishery products originating in the EU or in Kosovo.\n\n\n\n2.\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0The term \u201cagricultural and fishery products\u201d refers to the products listed in Chapters\u00a01 to\u00a024 of the Combined Nomenclature\n4\n and the products listed in Annex\u00a0I, paragraph\u00a0I, point\u00a0(ii) of the WTO Agreement on Agriculture.\n\n\n\n3.\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0This definition includes fish and fishery products covered by Chapter\u00a03, headings\u00a01604 (Prepared or preserved fish; caviar and caviar substitutes prepared from fish eggs) and\u00a01605 (Crustaceans, molluscs and other aquatic invertebrates, prepared or preserved (excl. smoked)), and subheadings\u00a00511\u00a091 (Fish waste), 2301\u00a020 (Flours, meals and pellets of fish or crustaceans, molluscs or other aquatic invertebrates, unfit for human consumption) and ex\u00a01902\u00a020 (\u201cstuffed pasta containing more than\u00a020\u00a0% by weight of fish, crustaceans, molluscs or other aquatic invertebrates\u201d).\n\n\n\nIt also includes the subheadings\u00a01212\u00a021\u00a000 (Seaweeds and other algae), ex\u00a01603\u00a000 (Extracts and juices of fish or crustaceans, molluscs or other aquatic invertebrates) and ex\u00a02309\u00a09010 (Preparations of a kind used in animal feeding: fish solubles), as well as\u00a01504\u00a010 and\u00a01504\u00a020 (fats and oils and their fractions, of fish, whether or not refined, but not chemically modified):\n\n\n\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0Fishliver oils and their fractions;\n\n\n\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0Fats and oils and their fractions, of fish, other than liver oils).\n\n\n\nARTICLE 27\n\n\n\nProcessed agricultural products\n\n\n\nProtocol\u00a0I lays down the trade arrangements for processed agricultural products which are listed therein.\n\n\n\n\n\n\nARTICLE 28\n\n\n\nEU concessions on imports of agricultural products originating in Kosovo\n\n\n\n1.\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0From the date of entry into force of this Agreement, the EU shall abolish all quantitative restrictions and measures having equivalent effect, on imports of agricultural products originating in Kosovo.\n\n\n\n2.\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0From the date of entry into force of this Agreement, the EU shall abolish the customs duties and charges having equivalent effect, on imports of agricultural products originating in Kosovo other than those of headings\u00a00102 (live bovine animals), 0201, (Meat of bovine animals, fresh or chilled) 0202 (Meat of bovine animals, frozen), 1701 (Cane or beet sugar and chemically pure sucrose, in solid form), 1702 (Other sugars, including chemically pure lactose, maltose, glucose and fructose, in solid form; sugar syrups not containing added flavouring or colouring matter; artificial honey, whether or not mixed with natural honey; caramel) and\u00a02204 (Wine of fresh grapes, including fortified wines; grape must other than that of heading\u00a02009) of the Combined Nomenclature.\n\n\n\nFor the products covered by Chapters\u00a07 and\u00a08 of the Combined Nomenclature, for which the Common Customs Tariff provides for the application of ad valorem customs duties and a specific customs duty, the elimination shall apply only to the ad valorem part of the duty.\n\n\n\n3.\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0From the date of entry into force of this Agreement, the EU shall fix the customs duties applicable to imports into the EU of \u201cbaby beef\u201d products defined in Annex\u00a0II and originating in Kosovo at\u00a020\u00a0% of the ad valorem duty and\u00a020\u00a0% of the specific duty as laid down in the Common Customs Tariff, within the limit of an annual tariff quota of\u00a0475 tonnes expressed in carcass weight.\n\n\n\nARTICLE 29\n\n\n\nKosovo\u2019s concessions on agricultural products\n\n\n\n1.\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0From the date of entry into force of this Agreement, Kosovo shall abolish all quantitative restrictions and measures having equivalent effect, on imports of agricultural products originating in the EU.\n\n\n\n2.\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0From the date of entry into force of this Agreement, Kosovo shall:\n\n\n\n\n\n(a)\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0abolish the customs duties applicable to imports of certain agricultural products originating in the EU, other than those listed in Annex\u00a0III;\n\n\n\n(b)\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0abolish progressively the customs duties applicable to imports of certain agricultural products originating in the EU, listed in Annex\u00a0IIIa, IIIb and IIIc and in accordance with the timetable indicated in that Annex.\n\n\n\n3.\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0The duty applicable to certain products listed in Annex\u00a0IIId shall be the basic duty applied in Kosovo on\u00a031\u00a0December\u00a02013.\n\n\n\nARTICLE 30\n\n\n\nWine and spirit drinks Protocol\n\n\n\nThe arrangements applicable to the wine and spirit drinks products referred to in Protocol\u00a0II are laid down in that Protocol.\n\n\n\n\nARTICLE 31\n\n\n\nEU concessions on fish and fishery products\n\n\n\n1.\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0From the date of entry into force of this Agreement, the EU shall abolish all quantitative restrictions and measures having equivalent effect on imports of fish and fishery products originating in Kosovo.\n\n\n\n2.\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0From the entry into force of this Agreement, the EU shall eliminate all customs duties and measures having equivalent effect on fish and fishery products originating in Kosovo other than those listed in Annex\u00a0IV. Products listed in Annex\u00a0IV shall be subject to the provisions laid down therein.\n\n\n\nARTICLE 32\n\n\n\n\n\nKosovo\u2019s concessions on fish and fishery products\n\n\n\n1.\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0From the date of entry into force of this Agreement, Kosovo shall abolish all quantitative restrictions and measures having equivalent effect on imports of fish and fishery products originating in the EU.\n\n\n\n2.\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0From the entry into force of this Agreement, Kosovo shall eliminate all customs duties and measures having equivalent effect on fish and fishery products originating in the EU other than those listed in Annex\u00a0V. Products listed in Annex\u00a0V shall be subject to the provisions laid down therein.\n\n\n\nARTICLE 33\n\n\n\nReview clause\n\n\n\nTaking account of the volume of trade in agricultural and fishery products between the Parties, of their particular sensitivities, of the rules of the EU common policies and of the policies for agriculture and fisheries in Kosovo, of the role of agriculture and fisheries in the economy of Kosovo, as well as developments in the framework of the WTO, the SAC shall examine, no later than three years after the entry into force of this Agreement, product by product and on an orderly and appropriate reciprocal basis, the opportunities for granting each other further concessions with a view to implementing greater liberalisation of the trade in agricultural and fishery products.\n\n\n\nARTICLE 34\n\n\n\nSafeguard clause \nconcerning agriculture and fisheries\n\n\n\nNotwithstanding other provisions of this Agreement, and in particular Article\u00a043, given the particular sensitivity of the agricultural and fisheries markets, if imports of products originating in one Party, which are the subject of concessions granted pursuant to Articles\u00a027, 28, 29, 30, 31 and\u00a032 cause serious disturbance to the markets or to the domestic regulatory mechanisms of either Party, the Parties shall enter into consultations immediately within the Stabilisation and Association Committee to find an appropriate solution. Pending such solution, the Party concerned may take the appropriate measures it deems necessary.\n\n\n\nARTICLE 35\n\n\n\nProtection of geographical indications \nfor agriculture and fishery products and foodstuffs \nother than wine and spirit drinks\n\n\n\n\n\n1.\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0Kosovo shall provide protection for the geographical indications of the EU registered in the EU under Regulation (EU) No\u00a01151/2012 of the European Parliament and of the Council of\u00a021\u00a0November\u00a02012 on quality schemes for agricultural products and foodstuffs\n5\n, in accordance with the terms laid down in this Article. Geographical indications of Kosovo shall be eligible for registration in the EU under the conditions set out in that Regulation.\n\n\n\n2.\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0The geographical indications referred to in paragraph\u00a01 shall be protected against:\n\n\n\n(a)\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0any direct or indirect commercial use of a protected name:\n\n\n\n(i)\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0for comparable products not compliant with the product specification of the protected name, or\n\n\n\n(ii)\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0in so far as such use exploits the reputation of a geographical indication;\n\n\n\n(b)\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0any misuse, imitation or evocation, even if the true origin of the product or service is indicated or if the protected name is translated or accompanied by an expression such as \u201cstyle\u201d, \u201ctype\u201d, \u201cmethod\u201d, \u201cas produced in\u201d, \u201cimitation\u201d, \u201cflavour\u201d, \u201clike\u201d or similar;\n\n\n\n(c)\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0any other false or misleading indication as to the provenance, origin, nature or essential qualities of the product, on the inner or outer packaging, advertising material or documents relating to that product, and the packing of the product in a container liable to convey a false impression as to its origin;\n\n\n\n(d)\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0any other practice liable to mislead the consumer as to the true origin of a like product.\n\n\n\n3.\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0A name proposed for registration that is wholly or partially homonymous with a name already protected, shall not be protected unless there is sufficient distinction in practice between the conditions of local and traditional usage and presentation of the homonym protected subsequently and the name already protected, taking into account the need to ensure equitable treatment of the producers concerned and that consumers are not misled. A homonymous name which misleads the consumer into believing that products come from another territory shall not be registered even if the name is accurate as far as the actual territory, region or place of origin of the products in question is concerned.\n\n\n\n4.\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0Kosovo shall refuse the registration of a trade mark the use of which corresponds to the situations referred to in paragraph\u00a02.\n\n\n\n5.\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0Trade marks the use of which corresponds to the situations referred to in paragraph\u00a02, which have been registered in Kosovo or established by use, shall no longer be used five years after the entry into force of this Agreement. However, this shall not apply to trade marks registered in Kosovo and trade marks established by use which are owned by nationals of third countries, provided they are not of such a nature as to deceive in any way the public as to the quality, the specification and the geographical origin of the goods.\n\n\n\n\n\n6.\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0Any use of the geographical indications protected in accordance with paragraph\u00a01 as terms customary in common language as the common name for such goods, or for products that have been legally marketed with that term in Kosovo, shall cease at the latest five years after the entry into force of this Agreement.\n\n\n\n7.\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0Kosovo shall ensure that goods exported from its territory five years after the entry into force of this Agreement do not infringe this Article.\n\n\n\n8.\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0Kosovo shall ensure the protection referred to in paragraphs\u00a01 to\u00a07 on its own initiative as well as at the request of an interested party.\n\n\n\nCHAPTER III\n\n\n\nCOMMON PROVISIONS\n\n\n\n\nARTICLE 36\n\n\n\nScope\n\n\n\nThis Chapter shall apply to trade in all products between the Parties except where otherwise provided in this Chapter or in Protocol\u00a0I.\n\n\n\n\nARTICLE 37\n\n\n\nImproved concessions\n\n\n\n\n\nThis Title shall in no way affect the application, on a unilateral basis, of more favourable measures by either Party.\n\n\n\nARTICLE 38\n\n\n\nStandstill\n\n\n\n1.\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0From the date of entry into force of this Agreement, no new customs duties on imports or exports or charges having equivalent effect shall be introduced, nor shall those already applied be increased, in trade between the EU and Kosovo.\n\n\n\n2.\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0From the date of entry into force of this Agreement, no new quantitative restriction on imports or exports or measure having equivalent effect shall be introduced, nor shall those existing be made more restrictive, in trade between the EU and Kosovo.\n\n\n\n3.\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0Without prejudice to the concessions granted under Articles\u00a028, 29, 30, 31 and\u00a032, paragraphs\u00a01 and\u00a02 of this Article shall not restrict in any way the pursuit of the respective agricultural and fishery policies of the EU and of Kosovo and the taking of any measures under those policies in so far as the import regime in Annexes\u00a0II to V and Protocol\u00a0I is not affected.\n\n\n\nARTICLE 39\n\n\n\nProhibition of fiscal discrimination\n\n\n\n1.\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0The EU and Kosovo shall refrain from any measure or practice of an internal fiscal nature establishing, whether directly or indirectly, discrimination between the products of one Party and like products originating in the territory of the other Party. Where such a measure or practice already exists, the EU and Kosovo, as appropriate, shall repeal or abolish it.\n\n\n\n2.\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0Products exported to the territory of one of the Parties shall not benefit from repayment of internal indirect taxation in excess of the amount of indirect taxation imposed on them.\n\n\n\n\n\n\nARTICLE 40\n\n\n\nDuties of a fiscal nature\n\n\n\nThe provisions concerning the abolition of customs duties on imports shall also apply to customs duties of a fiscal nature.\n\n\n\nARTICLE 41\n\n\n\nCustoms unions, free trade areas, \ncrossborder/boundary arrangements\n\n\n\n1.\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0This Agreement shall not preclude the maintenance or establishment of customs unions, free trade areas or arrangements for border/boundary trade except in so far as they alter the trade arrangements provided for in this Agreement.\n\n\n\n2.\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0During the transitional period specified in Article\u00a020, this Agreement shall not affect the implementation of the specific preferential arrangements governing the movement of goods either laid down in border/boundary Agreements previously concluded between one or more Member\u00a0States and Kosovo or resulting from the bilateral Agreements specified in Title\u00a0III concluded by Kosovo in order to promote regional trade.\n\n\n\n3.\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0Consultations between the Parties shall take place within the SAC concerning the Agreements referred to in paragraphs\u00a01 and\u00a02 and, where requested, on other major issues related to their respective trade policies towards third countries. In particular in the event of a third country acceding to the EU, such consultations shall take place so as to ensure that account is taken of the mutual interests of the EU and Kosovo as set out in this Agreement.\n\n\n\nARTICLE 42\n\n\n\nDumping and subsidy\n\n\n\n1.\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0This Agreement shall not prevent any of the Parties from taking trade defence action in accordance with paragraph\u00a02 of this Article and with Article\u00a043.\n\n\n\n\n\n2.\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0If one of the Parties finds that dumping and/or countervailable subsidisation is taking place in trade with the other Party, that Party may take appropriate measures against this practice consistent with the WTO Agreement on Implementation of Article VI of the GATT\u00a01994 or the WTO Agreement on Subsidies and Countervailing Measures and the respective internal legislation related to those agreements.\n\n\n\n\nARTICLE 43\n\n\n\nSafeguards clause\n\n\n\n1.\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0The parties agree that the rules and principles of Article XIX GATT\u00a01994 and the WTO Agreement on Safeguards are applied.\n\n\n\n2.\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0Notwithstanding paragraph\u00a01, the importing Party may take appropriate bilateral safeguard measures under the conditions and in accordance with the procedures laid down in this Article, where any product of one Party is being imported into the territory of the other Party in such increased quantities and under such conditions as to cause or threaten to cause:\n\n\n\n(a)\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0serious injury to the domestic industry of like or directly competitive products in the territory of the importing Party; or\n\n\n\n(b)\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0serious disturbances in any sector of the economy or difficulties which could bring about serious deterioration in the economic situation of a region of the importing Party.\n\n\n\n3.\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0Bilateral safeguard measures directed at imports from the other Party shall not exceed what is necessary to remedy the problems, as defined in paragraph\u00a02, which have arisen as a result of application of this Agreement. The safeguard measure adopted shall consist of a suspension in the increase or in the reduction of the margins of preferences provided for under this Agreement for the product concerned up to a maximum limit corresponding to the basic duty referred to in Article\u00a020, paragraph\u00a04(a) and (b) and paragraph\u00a05, for the same product. Such measures shall contain clear elements progressively leading to their elimination at the end of the set period, at the latest, and shall not be taken for a period exceeding two years.\n\n\n\nIn very exceptional circumstances, measures may be extended for a further period of maximum two years. No bilateral safeguard measure shall be applied to the import of a product that has previously been subject to such a measure for a period of time equal to that during which such measure had been previously applied, provided that the period of nonapplication is at least two years since the expiry of the measure.\n\n\n\n4.\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0In the cases specified in this Article, before taking the measures provided for therein or, in the cases to which paragraph\u00a05(b) of this Article applies, as soon as possible, the EU or Kosovo shall supply the SAC with all relevant information required for a thorough examination of the situation, with a view to seeking a solution acceptable to the Parties.\n\n\n\n5.\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0For the implementation of the paragraphs\u00a01, 2, 3 and\u00a04 the following provisions shall apply:\n\n\n\n\n\n(a)\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0The problems arising from the situation referred to in this Article shall be immediately referred for examination to the SAC, which may take any decisions needed to put an end to such problems.\n\n\n\nIf the SAC or the exporting Party has not taken a decision putting an end to the problems, or no other satisfactory solution has been reached within\u00a030 days of the matter being referred to the SAC, the importing Party may adopt the appropriate measures to remedy the problem in accordance with this Article. In the selection of safeguard measures, priority must be given to those which least disturb the functioning of the arrangements established in this Agreement. Safeguard measures shall preserve the level/margin of preference granted under this Agreement.\n\n\n\n(b)\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0Where exceptional and critical circumstances requiring immediate action make prior information or examination, as the case may be, impossible, the Party concerned may, in the situations specified in this Article, apply forthwith provisional measures necessary to deal with the situation and shall inform the other Party immediately thereof.\n\n\n\nThe safeguard measures shall be notified immediately to the SAC and shall be the subject of periodic consultations within that body, particularly with a view to establishing a timetable for their abolition as soon as circumstances so permit.\n\n\n\n6.\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0In the event of the EU, or Kosovo, subjecting imports of products liable to give rise to the problems referred to in this Article to an administrative procedure having as its purpose the rapid provision of information on the trend of trade flows, it shall inform the other Party.\n\n\n\nARTICLE 44\n\n\n\nShortage clause\n\n\n\n1.\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0Where compliance with this Title leads to:\n\n\n\n(a)\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0critical shortage, or threat thereof, of foodstuffs or other products essential to the exporting Party; or\n\n\n\n(b)\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0reexport to a third country of a product against which the exporting Party maintains quantitative export restrictions, export duties or measures or charges having equivalent effect, and where the situations referred to above give rise, or are likely to give rise to major difficulties for the exporting Party,\n\n\n\nthat Party may take appropriate measures under the conditions and in accordance with the procedures laid down in this Article.\n\n\n\n\n\n2.\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0In the selection of measures, priority must be given to those which least disturb the functioning of the arrangements in this Agreement. Such measures shall not be applied in a manner which would constitute a means of arbitrary or unjustifiable discrimination where the same conditions prevail, or a disguised restriction on trade, and shall be eliminated when conditions no longer justify their maintenance.\n\n\n\n3.\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0Before taking the measures provided for in paragraph\u00a01 or, as soon as possible in cases to which paragraph\u00a04 applies, the EU or Kosovo shall supply the SAC with all relevant information, with a view to seeking a solution acceptable to the Parties. The SAC may agree on any means needed to put an end to the difficulties. If no agreement is reached within\u00a030 days of the matter being referred to the SAC, the exporting Party may apply measures under this Article on the exportation of the product concerned.\n\n\n\n4.\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0Where exceptional and critical circumstances requiring immediate action make prior information or examination, as the case may be, impossible, the EU or Kosovo may apply forthwith the precautionary measures necessary to deal with the situation and shall inform the other Party immediately thereof.\n\n\n\n5.\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0Any measures applied pursuant to this Article shall be immediately notified to the SAC and shall be the subject of periodic consultations within that body, particularly with a view to establishing a timetable for their elimination as soon as circumstances so permit.\n\n\n\n\nARTICLE 45\n\n\n\nState monopolies\n\n\n\nWith regard to state monopolies of a commercial character, Kosovo shall ensure that, by the entry into force of this Agreement, no discrimination regarding the conditions under which goods are procured and marketed exists between nationals of the Member\u00a0States and Kosovo citizens.\n\n\n\n\nARTICLE 46\n\n\n\nRules of origin\n\n\n\nExcept as otherwise stipulated in this Agreement, Protocol\u00a0III lays down the rules of origin for the implementation of this Agreement.\n\n\n\n\n\nARTICLE 47\n\n\n\nRestrictions authorised\n\n\n\nThis Agreement shall not preclude prohibitions or restrictions on imports, exports or goods in transit justified on grounds of public morality, public policy or public security; the protection of health and life of humans, animals or plants; the protection of treasures of artistic, historic or archaeological value or the protection of intellectual, industrial and commercial property, or rules relating to gold and silver. Such prohibitions or restrictions shall not, however, constitute a means of arbitrary discrimination or a disguised restriction on trade between the Parties.\n\n\n\n\nARTICLE 48\n\n\n\nFailure to provide administrative cooperation\n\n\n\n1.\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0The Parties agree that administrative cooperation is essential for the implementation and the control of the preferential treatment granted under this Title and underline their commitment to combating irregularities and fraud in customs and related matters.\n\n\n\n2.\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0Where a Party has made a finding, on the basis of objective information, of a failure to provide administrative cooperation and/or of irregularities or fraud under this Title, that Party (referred to in this Article as \u201cthe Party concerned\u201d) may temporarily suspend the relevant preferential treatment of the product(s) concerned in accordance with this Article.\n\n\n\n3.\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0For the purpose of this Article a failure to provide administrative cooperation means, inter alia:\n\n\n\n(a)\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0a repeated failure to respect the obligations to verify the originating status of the product(s) concerned;\n\n\n\n(b)\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0a repeated refusal or undue delay in carrying out and/or communicating the results of subsequent verification of the proof of origin;\n\n\n\n\n\n(c)\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0a repeated refusal or undue delay in obtaining authorisation to conduct administrative cooperation missions to verify the authenticity of documents or accuracy of information relevant to the granting of the preferential treatment in question.\n\n\n\nFor the purpose of this Article, a finding of irregularities or fraud may be made, inter alia, where there is a rapid increase, without satisfactory explanation, in imports of goods exceeding the usual level of production and export capacity of the other Party, which is linked to objective information concerning irregularities or fraud.\n\n\n\n4.\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0The application of a temporary suspension shall be subject to the following conditions:\n\n\n\n(a)\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0the Party which has made a finding, on the basis of objective information, of a failure to provide administrative cooperation and/or of irregularities or fraud shall immediately notify the Stabilisation and Association Committee of its finding, together with the objective information, and enter into consultations with the other Party within the Stabilisation and Association Committee, on the basis of all relevant information and objective findings, with a view to reaching a solution acceptable to both Parties.\n\n\n\n(b)\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0Where the Parties have entered into consultations within the Stabilisation and Association Committee under point\u00a0(a) and have failed to agree on an acceptable solution within three months following the notification, the Party concerned may temporarily suspend the relevant preferential treatment of the product(s) concerned. A temporary suspension shall be notified to the Stabilisation and Association Committee immediately.\n\n\n\n(c)\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0Temporary suspensions under this Article shall be limited to the minimum necessary to protect the financial interests of the Party concerned. They shall not exceed a period of six months, which may be renewed. Temporary suspensions shall be notified immediately after their adoption to the Stabilisation and Association Committee. They shall be subject to periodic consultations within the Stabilisation and Association Committee, in particular with a view to their termination as soon as the conditions for their application no longer prevail.\n\n\n\n5.\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0At the same time as the notification to the Stabilisation and Association Committee under paragraph\u00a04(a), the Party concerned shall publish a notice to importers in its Official Journal. The notice to importers should indicate for the product concerned that there is a finding, on the basis of objective information, of a failure to provide administrative cooperation and/or of irregularities or fraud.\n\n\n\n\nARTICLE 49\n\n\n\nIn case of error by the competent authorities in the proper management of the preferential system at export, and in particular in the application of Protocol\u00a0III where this error leads to consequences in terms of import duties, the Contracting Party facing such consequences may request the SAC to examine the possibilities of adopting all appropriate measures with a view to resolving the situation.\n\n\n\nTITLE V\n\n\n\nESTABLISHMENT, \nSUPPLY OF SERVICES AND CAPITAL\n\n\n\n\n\n\nARTICLE 50\n\n\n\nDefinition\n\n\n\nFor the purposes of this Agreement:\n\n\n\n(1)\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u201cEU company\u201d and \u201cKosovo company\u201d means, respectively, a company set up in accordance with the laws of a Member\u00a0State, or of Kosovo, and having its registered office or central administration or principal place of business in the territory of the EU or of Kosovo. However, should the company have only its registered office in the territory of the EU or of Kosovo respectively, the company shall be considered an EU or a Kosovo company if its operations possess a real and continuous link with the economy of one of the Member\u00a0States or of Kosovo;\n\n\n\n(2)\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u201cSubsidiary\u201d of a company means a company which is effectively controlled by another company;\n\n\n\n(3)\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u201cBranch\u201d of a company means a place of business not having legal personality which has the appearance of permanency, such as the extension of a parent body, has a management and is materially equipped to negotiate business with third parties so that the latter, although knowing that there will, where necessary, be a legal link with the parent body, the head office of which is abroad, do not have to deal directly with such parent body but may transact business at the place of business constituting the extension;\n\n\n\n(4)\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u201cEstablishment\u201d means the right to take up economic activities by means of the setting up of companies including subsidiaries and branches in the EU or in Kosovo respectively;\n\n\n\n(5)\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u201cOperations\u201d means the pursuit of economic activities;\n\n\n\n(6)\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u201cEconomic activities\u201d in principle includes activities of an industrial, commercial or professional character and activities of craftsmen;\n\n\n\n(7)\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u201cEU national\u201d and \u201ccitizen of Kosovo\u201d means respectively a natural person who is a national of a Member\u00a0State or a citizen of Kosovo;\n\n\n\n\n\n(8)\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u201cFinancial services\u201d means the activities described in Annex\u00a0VI.\n\n\n\nCHAPTER I\n\n\n\nESTABLISHMENT\n\n\n\n\nARTICLE 51\n\n\n\n1.\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0Kosovo shall facilitate the setting up of operations on its territory by EU companies. To that end, Kosovo shall grant, upon entry into force of this Agreement:\n\n\n\n(a)\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0as regards the establishment of EU companies on the territory of Kosovo, treatment no less favourable than that accorded to its own companies or to any third country company, whichever is the better;\n\n\n\n(b)\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0as regards the operation of subsidiaries and branches of EU companies on the territory of Kosovo once established, treatment no less favourable than that accorded to its own companies and branches or to any subsidiary and branch of any third country company, whichever is the better.\n\n\n\n2.\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0The EU shall grant, from the entry into force of this Agreement:\n\n\n\n(a)\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0as regards the establishment of Kosovo companies treatment no less favourable than that accorded by the EU to its own companies or to any company of any third country, whichever is the better;\n\n\n\n(b)\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0as regards the operation of subsidiaries and branches of Kosovo companies, established in its territory, treatment no less favourable than that accorded by the EU to its own companies and branches, or to any subsidiary and branch of any third country company, established in its territory, whichever is the better.\n\n\n\n3.\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0The Parties shall not adopt any new regulations or measures which introduce discrimination as regards the establishment of the other Party\u2019s companies on their territory or in respect of their operation, once established, by comparison with their own companies.\n\n\n\n\n\n4.\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0Notwithstanding this Article,\n\n\n\n(a)\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0subsidiaries and branches of EU companies shall have, from the entry into force of this Agreement, the right to use and rent real property in Kosovo;\n\n\n\n(b)\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0subsidiaries and branches of EU companies shall, within five years from the entry into force of this Agreement, have the right to acquire and enjoy ownership rights over real property as Kosovo companies and, as regards public goods/goods of common interest, the same rights as enjoyed by Kosovo companies respectively where these rights are necessary for the conduct of the economic activities for which they are established.\n\n\n\n\nARTICLE 52\n\n\n\n1.\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0Subject to Article\u00a054 the Parties may regulate the establishment and operation of companies on their territory, insofar as these regulations do not discriminate against companies of the other Party in comparison with its own companies.\n\n\n\n2.\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0In respect of financial services, notwithstanding any other provisions of this Agreement, a Party shall not be prevented from taking measures for prudential reasons, including for the protection of investors, depositors, policy holders or persons to whom a fiduciary duty is owed by a financial service supplier, or to ensure the integrity and stability of the financial system. Such measures shall not be used as a means of avoiding the Party\u2019s obligations under this Agreement.\n\n\n\n3.\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0Nothing in this Agreement shall be construed to require a Party to disclose information relating to the affairs and accounts of individual customers or any confidential or proprietary information in the possession of public entities.\n\n\n\n\nARTICLE 53\n\n\n\n1.\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0This Chapter is without prejudice to provisions of the Transport Community Treaty with the Western Balkans and of the Multilateral Agreement on the establishment of the European Common Aviation Area signed on\u00a09\u00a0June\u00a02006\n6\n.\n\n\n\n2.\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0Within the scope of the EU transport policy, the SAC may make recommendations in specific cases for improving establishment and operations in the areas covered by paragraph\u00a01.\n\n\n\n\n\n3.\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0This Chapter shall not apply to maritime transport.\n\n\n\nARTICLE 54\n\n\n\n1.\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0Articles\u00a051 and\u00a052 do not preclude the application by a Party of particular rules concerning the establishment and operation in its territory of branches of companies of another Party not incorporated in the territory of the first Party, which are justified by legal or technical differences between such branches as compared to branches of companies incorporated in its territory or, as regards financial services, for prudential reasons.\n\n\n\n2.\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0The difference in treatment shall not go beyond what is strictly necessary as a result of such legal or technical differences or, as regards financial services, for prudential reasons.\n\n\n\nCHAPTER II\n\n\n\nSUPPLY OF SERVICES\n\n\n\n\nARTICLE 55\n\n\n\n1.\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0An EU company established in the territory of Kosovo or a Kosovo company established in the EU shall be entitled to employ, or have employed by one of its subsidiaries or branches, in accordance with the legislation in force in the host territory of establishment, in the territory of the EU and of Kosovo respectively, employees who are nationals of the EU or citizens of Kosovo respectively, provided that such employees are key personnel as defined in paragraph\u00a02 and that they are employed exclusively by companies, subsidiaries or branches.\n\n\n\n2.\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0Key personnel of the abovementioned companies hereinafter referred to as \u201corganisations\u201d are \u201cintracorporate transferees\u201d as defined in point\u00a0(c) in the following categories, provided that the
